NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

R. Jayabalan born as a male child to Rajanthran born on 11th October 1973 residing at Devaanbu Illam, Mela Street,
Mettuppatty, Lalgudi Taluk, Tiruchirappalli-621 706. After the biological change has been living as a female (Reference
Dr. V. Jayaraman, Plastic Surgen, Government Kilpauk Medical College Hospital, Kilpauk, Chennai-10.) The clinical
Examination under the reference above also shows that I could be treated as a female. Hence R. Jayabalan shall henceforth
be known as R. JAYAMALINI.
Tiruchirappalli, 27th June 2011.

R. JAYABALAN.

Tiruchirappalli-620 006, after the biological change has been living as a female (Dr. K.V. Alala Sundaram, Plastic Surgen,
Madras Medical College and Government General Hospital, Chennai-600 003.) The clinical examination under the reference
above also shows that I could be treated as a female. Hence R. Kannan, shall henceforth be known as R. SWETHA.
Tiruchirappalli, 27th June 2011.

R. KANNAN.

as K. MAHESWARI.
